<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:joelen.html>joelen</a> (82395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a> (859)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jonc</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:jung.html>jung</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:jung.html>jung</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jungaz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂yuh₁n̥ḱós</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jong.html>jong</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jonger.html>jonger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">jongst</b>)

***juf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:juf.html>juf</a> (8260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Clipping <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:juffrouw.html>juffrouw</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 19th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:juicht.html>juicht</a> (29248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:juicht.html>juicht</a></strong>
</p>
